FROM `od_user` as `a`
JOIN `od_partner_mod` as `b` ON `a`.`id`=`b`.`user_id`
JOIN `od_partner` as `c` ON `b`.`partner_id`=`c`.`partner_id`
JOIN `od_partner_bank` as `d` ON `c`.`partner_id`=`d`.`partner_id`
